Wait for AirSim window  loading completely and then kill the roslaunch process in terminal. Run airsim_sim.launch again to normally launch AirSim simulation.</div><div style="position: relative; left: 0px;"></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div data-block-id="2a63a108-5f43-47a2-8834-3fd6418f170c" class="notion-selectable notion-numbered_list-block" style="width: 100%;
